focus_tree = {
	id = Syria_2000
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			AND = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = SYR
					original_tag = FSA
					original_tag = NUS
				}
			}
		}
	}
	default = no

	shared_focus = SYR_diplomatic_effort
	shared_focus = SYR_greater_syria
	shared_focus = SYR_military_reform

	continuous_focus_position = { x = 1300 y = 1700 }

	#Main succession branch
	focus = {
		id = SYR_death_of_hafez_al_assad
		icon = national_unity_red
		cost = 10
		x = 9
		y = 0

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		available = {
			always = no
		}

		bypass = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TT_DEATH_OF_HAFEZ
				has_country_flag = Syria_Hafez_dead
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_death_of_hafez_al_assad"
		}

	}
	##Bushra's branch
	focus = {
		id = SYR_bushra_al_assad
		icon = Bushra_al_Assad
		cost = 5
		prerequisite = {
			focus = SYR_death_of_hafez_al_assad
		}
		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = SYR_bashar_al_assad
			focus = SYR_maher_al_assad
			focus = SYR_flowers_of_damascus_spring
		}
		x = 3
		y = 1

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1.9
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				OR = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { bushra_popularity > bashar_popularity }
						check_variable = { bushra_popularity > maher_popularity }
					}
					neutrality > 0.4
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}

		available = {
			emerging_autocracy_are_in_power = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Syrian_rebels }
		}

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_bushra_al_assad"
			hidden_effect = { kill_country_leader = yes }
			clear_array = ruling_party
			clear_array = gov_coalition_array
			add_to_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
			add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 7 }
			add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 13 }
			add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 18 }
			add_to_array = { gov_coalition_array = 19 }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Bushra al-Assad"
				picture = "Bushra_Al-Assad.dds"
				ideology = oligarchism
				traits = {
					neutrality_oligarchism
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { max_leader = bushra_popularity }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { max_leader < bashar_popularity } }
				set_temp_variable = { max_leader = bashar_popularity }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { max_leader < maher_popularity } }
				set_temp_variable = { max_leader = maher_popularity }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { stability_loss = bushra_popularity }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { stability_loss = max_leader }
			divide_temp_variable = { stability_loss = 100 }
			add_stability = stability_loss
			set_temp_variable = { leader_popularity = bushra_popularity }
			divide_temp_variable = { leader_popularity = 200 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = leader_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { var = party_pop_array^15 value = leader_popularity }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
			}
			recalculate_party = yes
			set_country_flag = Syria_successor_chosen
		}

	}

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { max_leader < bashar_popularity } }
				set_temp_variable = { max_leader = bashar_popularity }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { max_leader < maher_popularity } }
				set_temp_variable = { max_leader = maher_popularity }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { stability_loss = maher_popularity }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { stability_loss = max_leader }
			divide_temp_variable = { stability_loss = 100 }
			add_stability = stability_loss
			set_temp_variable = { leader_popularity = maher_popularity }
			divide_temp_variable = { leader_popularity = 200 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = leader_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { var = party_pop_array^22 value = leader_popularity }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = nationalist
			}
			recalculate_party = yes
			set_country_flag = Syria_successor_chosen
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1.9
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				OR = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { maher_popularity > bashar_popularity }
						check_variable = { maher_popularity > bushra_popularity }
					}
					nationalist > 0.4
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

shared_focus = {
	id = SYR_deal_with_scraps
	icon = lebonan_resistance
	cost = 10
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SYR_lebanese_chaos
	}
	x = -9
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = SYR_greater_syria

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			any_neighbor_country = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	available = {
		has_government = nationalist
		is_subject = no
		OR = {
			AND = {
				country_exists = LEB
				NOT = { country_exists = HEZ }
			}
			AND = {
				country_exists = HEZ
				NOT = { country_exists = LEB }
			}
		}
	}

	bypass = {
		NOT = { country_exists = LEB }
		NOT = { country_exists = HEZ }
	}

	cancel_if_invalid = yes


	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_deal_with_scraps"
		if = {
			limit = { LEB = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			every_core_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = LEB }
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			annex_country = { target = LEB transfer_troops = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { HEZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			annex_country = { target = HEZ transfer_troops = yes }
			every_core_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = HEZ }
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { country_exists = LEB }
			LEB = { country_event = { id = SyriaFocus.52 hours = 6 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { country_exists = HEZ }
			HEZ = { country_event = { id = SyriaFocus.52 hours = 6 } }
		}
	}

}

shared_focus = {
	id = SYR_assault_jordan
	icon = anti_monarchism2
	cost = 10
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SYR_lebanese_chaos
	}
	x = -7
	y = 3
	relative_position_id = SYR_greater_syria

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			any_neighbor_country = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	available = {
		has_government = nationalist
		is_subject = no
		country_exists = JOR
		NOT = { is_in_faction_with = JOR }
	}

	bypass = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { country_exists = JOR }
			JOR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
		}
	}

	will_lead_to_war_with = JOR

	cancel_if_invalid = yes


	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_assault_jordan"
		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_SYR_ASSAULT_JORDAN
		set_temp_variable = { success_chance = JOR.party_popularity@nationalist }
		multiply_temp_variable = { success_chance = 200 }
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = success_chance
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { remaining_chance = 100 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { remaining_chance = success_chance }
		set_temp_variable = { civil_war_chance = remaining_chance }
		multiply_temp_variable = { civil_war_chance = 0.5 }
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = civil_war_chance
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { remaining_chance = civil_war_chance }
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = remaining_chance
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = success_chance
				}
				JOR = { country_event = SyriaFocus.55 }
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = civil_war_chance
				}
				JOR = { country_event = SyriaFocus.57 }
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = remaining_chance
				}
				JOR = { country_event = SyriaFocus.58 }
			}
		}
	}

}

		NOT = { has_war_with = IRQ }

		}

				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { KUR = { exists = yes } }
			KUR = {
				every_owned_state = {
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { IRQ = { has_idea = sunni } }
			if = {
				limit = { IRQ = { NOT = { has_government = communism } } }
				IRQ = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = communism
						size = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { IRQ = { has_government = communism } }
				IRQ = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = nationalist
						size = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = IRQ
						NOT = { tag = IRQ }
					}
					remove_ideas = sunni
					add_ideas = shia
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { IRQ = { has_idea = shia } }
			if = {
				limit = { IRQ = { NOT = { has_government = nationalist } } }
				IRQ = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = nationalist
						size = 0.3
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { IRQ = { has_government = nationalist } }
				IRQ = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = communism
						size = 0.3
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = IRQ
						NOT = { tag = IRQ }
					}
					remove_ideas = shia
					add_ideas = sunni
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { IRQ = { country_event = SyriaFocus.65 } }
	}

		custom_effect_tooltip = TT_SYR_CONCESSIONS_TO_KURDS
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { ROJ = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = KUR }
					KUR = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROJ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				KUR = { annex_country = { target = ROJ transfer_troops = yes } }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = KUR
							is_core_of = ROJ
						}
					}
					KUR = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = KUR }
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

shared_focus = {
	id = SYR_meet_hamas
	icon = align_to_hamas
	cost = 10
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SYR_affirm_claims_on_golan
	}
	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = SYR_meet_fatah
	}
	x = -10
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = SYR_diplomatic_effort

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_historical_focus_on = yes
		}
	}

	available = {
		OR = {
			country_exists = HAM
			country_exists = PAL
		}
		OR = {
			HAM = { owns_state = 209 }
			PAL = { owns_state = 209 }
		}
	}

	bypass = {
	}

	cancel_if_invalid = yes


	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INFLUENCE }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_meet_hamas"
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { country_exists = HAM } }
			209 = { add_core_of = HAM }
			PAL = { release = HAM }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = PAL }
					add_core_of = HAM
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = PAL }
					add_claim_by = HAM
				}
				HAM = { load_oob = HAM_2017 }
				ISR = {
					remove_state_claim = 209
					add_state_core = 209
				}
				PAL = {
					add_state_core = 209
				}
			}
			ISR = { country_event = { id = SyriaFocus.76 hours = 6 } }
			PAL = { country_event = { id = SyriaFocus.76 hours = 6 } }
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = HAM
			modifier = declaration_of_friendship
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = HAM
			modifier = declaration_of_friendship
		}
		HAM = {
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ROOT.id }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS.id }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
		}
	}

}

			USA = { has_country_flag = war_on_terror_speech }
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = fascism
			has_government = neutrality
			has_start_date < 2016.1.1
		}
		is_subject = no
	}

	bypass = {
		has_idea = global_salafist_recruitment
	}

	cancel_if_invalid = yes


	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_harbor_extremists"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 11 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.1 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.1 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
	}

}

shared_focus = {
	id = SYR_release_extremists
	icon = isis_tahrir_alliance
	cost = 10
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SYR_harbor_extremists
	}
	x = 23
	y = 2
	relative_position_id = SYR_diplomatic_effort

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	cancel_if_invalid = yes


	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_release_extremists"
		every_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_idea = shia
						NOT = { original_tag = HEZ }
					}
					has_idea = sunni
					original_tag = LEB
					AND = {
						original_tag = HEZ
						NOT = { country_exists = LEB }
					}
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { threat_change = 5 }
			modify_terror_threat_effect = yes
		}
	}

}

shared_focus = {
	id = SYR_arm_palestinians
	icon = align_to_hamas
	cost = 10
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SYR_release_extremists
	}
	x = 23
	y = 3
	relative_position_id = SYR_diplomatic_effort

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}

	available = {
		OR = {
			country_exists = HAM
			country_exists = PAL
		}
		OR = {
			HAM = { owns_state = 209 }
			PAL = { owns_state = 209 }
		}
	}

	bypass = {
		NOT = { country_exists = HAM }
		NOT = { PAL = { owns_state = 209 } }
	}

	cancel_if_invalid = yes


	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INFLUENCE }
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SYR_arm_palestinians"
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { country_exists = HAM } }
			209 = { add_core_of = HAM }
			PAL = { release = HAM }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = PAL }
					add_core_of = HAM
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = PAL }
					add_claim_by = HAM
				}
				HAM = { load_oob = HAM_2017 }
			}
			ISR = { country_event = { id = SyriaFocus.76 hours = 6 } }
			PAL = { country_event = { id = SyriaFocus.76 hours = 6 } }
		}
		send_equipment = {
			equipment = Inf_equipment
			amount = 1000
			target = HAM
		}
		HAM = {
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ROOT.id }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS.id }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
		}
	}

}
